package_gnu="no"; \
test -n "$package_gnu" || { \
  if { if (LC_ALL=C find --version) 2>/dev/null | grep GNU >/dev/null; then \
	 LC_ALL=C find -L ../.. -maxdepth 1 -type f \
		       -size -10000000c -exec grep 'GNU geany' \
		       /dev/null '{}' ';' 2>/dev/null; \
       else \
	 LC_ALL=C grep 'GNU geany' ../../* 2>/dev/null; \
       fi; \
     } | grep -v 'libtool:' >/dev/null; then \
     package_gnu=yes; \
   else \
     package_gnu=no; \
   fi; \
}; \
if test "$package_gnu" = "yes"; then \
  package_prefix='GNU '; \
else \
  package_prefix=''; \
fi; \
if test -n 'https://github.com/geany/geany/issues' || test 'https://github.com/geany/geany/issues' = '@'PACKAGE_BUGREPORT'@'; then \
  msgid_bugs_address='https://github.com/geany/geany/issues'; \
else \
  msgid_bugs_address='https://github.com/geany/geany/issues'; \
fi; \

    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < ../../po/geany.pot > geany.1po && \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < geany.po > geany.2po && \
    if cmp geany.1po geany.2po >/dev/null 2>&1; then \

    fi; \

package_gnu="no"; \
test -n "$package_gnu" || { \
  if { if (LC_ALL=C find --version) 2>/dev/null | grep GNU >/dev/null; then \
	 LC_ALL=C find -L ../.. -maxdepth 1 -type f \
		       -size -10000000c -exec grep 'GNU geany' \
		       /dev/null '{}' ';' 2>/dev/null; \
       else \
	 LC_ALL=C grep 'GNU geany' ../../* 2>/dev/null; \
       fi; \
     } | grep -v 'libtool:' >/dev/null; then \
     package_gnu=yes; \
   else \
     package_gnu=no; \
   fi; \
}; \
if test "$package_gnu" = "yes"; then \
  package_prefix='GNU '; \
else \
  package_prefix=''; \
fi; \
if test -n 'https://github.com/geany/geany/issues' || test 'https://github.com/geany/geany/issues' = '@'PACKAGE_BUGREPORT'@'; then \
  msgid_bugs_address='https://github.com/geany/geany/issues'; \
else \
  msgid_bugs_address='https://github.com/geany/geany/issues'; \
fi; \
case `/usr/bin/xgettext --version | sed 1q | sed -e 's,^[^0-9]*,,'` in \
  '' | 0.[0-9] | 0.[0-9].* | 0.1[0-5] | 0.1[0-5].* | 0.16 | 0.16.[0-1]*) \
    /usr/bin/xgettext --default-domain=geany --directory=../.. \
      --add-comments=TRANSLATORS: --keyword=_ --keyword=N_ --keyword=C_:1c,2 --keyword=NC_:1c,2 --keyword=g_dngettext:2,3 --from-code=UTF-8 -c"Translators:"  \
      --files-from=../../po/POTFILES.in \
      --copyright-holder='The Geany contributors' \
      --msgid-bugs-address="$msgid_bugs_address" \
    ;; \
  *) \
    /usr/bin/xgettext --default-domain=geany --directory=../.. \
      --add-comments=TRANSLATORS: --keyword=_ --keyword=N_ --keyword=C_:1c,2 --keyword=NC_:1c,2 --keyword=g_dngettext:2,3 --from-code=UTF-8 -c"Translators:"  \
      --files-from=../../po/POTFILES.in \
      --copyright-holder='The Geany contributors' \
      --package-name="${package_prefix}geany" \
      --package-version='2.2.0' \
      --msgid-bugs-address="$msgid_bugs_address" \
    ;; \
esac
/usr/bin/xgettext: warning: a fallback ITS rule file '/usr/share/gettext-0.21/its/gtkbuilder.its' is used; it may not be in sync with the upstream
test ! -f geany.po || { \
  if test -f ../../po/geany.pot-header; then \
    sed -e '1,/^#$/d' < geany.po > geany.1po && \
    cat ../../po/geany.pot-header geany.1po > geany.po; \
    rm -f geany.1po; \
  fi; \
  if test -f ../../po/geany.pot; then \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < ../../po/geany.pot > geany.1po && \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < geany.po > geany.2po && \
    if cmp geany.1po geany.2po >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
      rm -f geany.1po geany.2po geany.po; \
    else \
      rm -f geany.1po geany.2po ../../po/geany.pot && \
      mv geany.po ../../po/geany.pot; \
    fi; \
  else \
    mv geany.po ../../po/geany.pot; \
  fi; \
}

package_gnu="no"; \
test -n "$package_gnu" || { \
  if { if (LC_ALL=C find --version) 2>/dev/null | grep GNU >/dev/null; then \
	 LC_ALL=C find -L ../../.. -maxdepth 1 -type f \
		       -size -10000000c -exec grep 'GNU geany' \
		       /dev/null '{}' ';' 2>/dev/null; \
       else \
	 LC_ALL=C grep 'GNU geany' ../../../* 2>/dev/null; \
       fi; \
     } | grep -v 'libtool:' >/dev/null; then \
     package_gnu=yes; \
   else \
     package_gnu=no; \
   fi; \
}; \
if test "$package_gnu" = "yes"; then \
  package_prefix='GNU '; \
else \
  package_prefix=''; \
fi; \

else \
  msgid_bugs_address='https://github.com/geany/geany/issues'; \
fi; \

test ! -f geany.po || { \
  if test -f ../../../po/geany.pot-header; then \
    sed -e '1,/^#$/d' < geany.po > geany.1po && \
    cat ../../../po/geany.pot-header geany.1po > geany.po; \
    rm -f geany.1po; \
  fi; \
  if test -f ../../../po/geany.pot; then \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < ../../../po/geany.pot > geany.1po && \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < geany.po > geany.2po && \
    if cmp geany.1po geany.2po >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
      rm -f geany.1po geany.2po geany.po; \
    else \
      rm -f geany.1po geany.2po ../../../po/geany.pot && \
      mv geany.po ../../../po/geany.pot; \
    fi; \
  else \
    mv geany.po ../../../po/geany.pot; \
  fi; \
}
